\subsection{Detailed Description}
This section details the Structures and Functions relavent to the T\+DI Engine~\newline
 For an example of how to connect to the device and perform simple operations use the following links\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Example of using the Thorlabs.Motion\+Control.T\+D\+I\+Engine.D\+LL from a C or C++ project.~\newline
 This requires the D\+LL to be dynamical linked.  
\item Example of using the Thorlabs.Motion\+Control.T\+D\+I\+Engine.D\+LL from a C\# project~\newline
 This uses Marshalling to load and access the C D\+LL.  
\end{DoxyItemize}The Thorlabs.\+Motion\+Control.\+T\+D\+I\+Engine.\+D\+LL requires the following D\+L\+Ls 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Thorlabs.\+Motion\+Control.\+Device\+Manager.  
\end{DoxyItemize}

Gets the hardware information from the device. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em serial\+No} & The device serial no. \\
\hline
{\em channel} & The channel. \\
\hline
{\em model\+No} & Address of a buffer to receive the model number string. Minimum 8 characters \\
\hline
{\em size\+Of\+Model\+No} & The size of the model number buffer, minimum of 8 characters. \\
\hline
{\em type} & Address of a W\+O\+RD to receive the hardware type number. \\
\hline
{\em num\+Channels} & Address of a short to receive the number of channels. \\
\hline
{\em notes} & Address of a buffer to receive the notes describing the device. \\
\hline
{\em size\+Of\+Notes} & The size of the notes buffer, minimum of 48 characters. \\
\hline
{\em firmware\+Version} & Address of a D\+W\+O\+RD to receive the firmware version number made up of 4 byte parts. \\
\hline
{\em hardware\+Version} & Address of a W\+O\+RD to receive the hardware version number. \\
\hline
{\em modification\+State} & Address of a W\+O\+RD to receive the hardware modification state number. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The error code (see Error Codes) or zero if successful. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{T\+D\+I\+\_\+\+Get\+Status\+Bits(char const $\ast$serial\+No, short channel)}{TDI_GetStatusBits(char const *serialNo, short channel)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}T\+D\+I\+E\+N\+G\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+A\+PI D\+W\+O\+RD \+\_\+\+\_\+cdecl T\+D\+I\+\_\+\+Get\+Status\+Bits (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\item[{short}]{channel}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{group___t_d_i_engine_gae1ff213190e734d01d39660972f176f0}{}\label{group___t_d_i_engine_gae1ff213190e734d01d39660972f176f0}


Get the current status bits. 

This returns the latest status bits received from the device.~\newline
 To get new status bits, use \hyperlink{group___t_d_i_engine_ga45c16bbd6acc7826f98464e96011a475}{T\+D\+I\+\_\+\+Request\+Status\+Bits(char const $\ast$ serial\+No, short channel)} or use the polling functions, \hyperlink{group___t_d_i_engine_ga7c22f7f8bb3689d79de383c0c7d5c0b1}{T\+D\+I\+\_\+\+Start\+Polling(char const $\ast$ serial\+No, short channel, int milliseconds)}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em channel} & The channel. \\
\hline
{\em serial\+No} & The device serial no. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The status bits from the device \tabulinesep=1mm
\begin{longtabu} spread 0pt [c]{*2{|X[-1]}|}
\hline
0x00000001&CW hardware limit switch (0=No contact, 1=Contact). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00000002&C\+CW hardware limit switch (0=No contact, 1=Contact). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00000004&CW software limit switch (0=No contact, 1=Contact). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00000008&C\+CW software limit switch (0=No contact, 1=Contact). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00000010&Motor shaft moving clockwise (1=Moving, 0=Stationary). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00000020&Motor shaft moving counterclockwise (1=Moving, 0=Stationary). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00000040&Shaft jogging clockwise (1=Moving, 0=Stationary). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00000080&Shaft jogging counterclockwise (1=Moving, 0=Stationary). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00000100&Motor connected (1=Connected, 0=Not connected). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00000200&Motor homing (1=Homing, 0=Not homing). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00000400&Motor homed (1=Homed, 0=Not homed). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00000800&For Future Use. \\\cline{1-2}
0x00001000&Trajectory within tracking window (1=Within window, 0=Not within window). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00002000&Axis within settled window (1=Settled within window, 0=Not settled within window). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00004000&Axis exceeds position error limit (1=Limit exceeded, 0=Within limit). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00008000&Set when position module instruction error exists (1=Instruction error exists, 0=No error). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00010000&Interlock link missing in motor connector (1=Missing, 0=Present). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00020000&Position module over temperature warning (1=Over temp, 0=Temp OK). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00040000&Position module bus voltage fault (1=Fault exists, 0=OK). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00080000&Axis commutation error (1=Error, 0=OK). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00100000&Digital input 1 state (1=Logic high, 0=Logic low). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00200000&Digital input 2 state (1=Logic high, 0=Logic low). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00400000&Digital input 3 state (1=Logic high, 0=Logic low). \\\cline{1-2}
0x00800000&Digital input 4 state (1=Logic high, 0=Logic low). \\\cline{1-2}
0x01000000&Axis phase current limit (1=Current limit exceeded, 0=Below limit). \\\cline{1-2}
0x02000000&Not used. \\\cline{1-2}
0x04000000&For Future Use. \\\cline{1-2}
0x08000000&For Future Use. \\\cline{1-2}
0x10000000&For Future Use. \\\cline{1-2}
0x20000000&Active (1=Active, 0=Not active). \\\cline{1-2}
0x40000000&For Future Use. \\\cline{1-2}
0x80000000&Channel enabled (1=Enabled, 0=Disabled). \\\cline{1-2}
\end{longtabu}


Bits 21 to 24 (Digital Input States) are only applicable if the associated digital input is fitted to your controller -\/ see the relevant handbook for more details. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{group___t_d_i_engine_ga45c16bbd6acc7826f98464e96011a475}{T\+D\+I\+\_\+\+Request\+Status\+Bits(char const $\ast$ serial\+No, short channel)}, \hyperlink{group___t_d_i_engine_ga7c22f7f8bb3689d79de383c0c7d5c0b1}{T\+D\+I\+\_\+\+Start\+Polling(char const $\ast$ serial\+No, short channel, int milliseconds)}


\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Sets the software limits mode. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em serial\+No} & The device serial no. \\
\hline
{\em channel} & The channel. \\
\hline
{\em limits\+Software\+Approach\+Policy} & The soft limit mode \begin{tabularx}{\linewidth}{|*{2}{>{\raggedright\arraybackslash}X|}}\hline
Disable any move outside travel range. &0 \\\cline{1-2}
Disable any move outside travel range, but allow moves \textquotesingle{}just beyond limit\textquotesingle{} to be truncated to limit. &1 \\\cline{1-2}
Truncate all moves beyond limit to the current limit. &2 \\\cline{1-2}
Allow all moves, illegal or not. &3 \\\cline{1-2}
\end{tabularx}
\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
If these are bitwise-\/\+O\+Red with 0x0080 then the limits are swapped.

Build the Device\+List. 

This function builds an internal collection of all devices found on the U\+SB that are not currently open. ~\newline
 N\+O\+TE, if a device is open, it will not appear in the list until the device has been closed. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The error code (see Error Codes) or zero if successful. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
